           <a aria-label="Some of those we lost in Windsor-Essex during the first year of COVID-19" class="article-card__link" href="/news/local-news/some-of-those-we-lost-in-windsor-essex-during-the-first-year-of-covid-19">
            <h3 class="article-card__headline" title="Some of those we lost in Windsor-Essex during the first year of COVID-19">
             <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
              Some of those we lost in Windsor-Essex during the first year of COVID-19
             </span>
            </h3>
            <p class="article-card__excerpt">
             Searching through news reports, public obituaries, and social media posts, the Star has compiled the following list of some community members who died as a result of COVID-19 in Windsor and Essex County in the first year of the pandemic. March 20 marks the one-year anniversary of the first confirmed case locally of COVID-19. This list is not comprehensive but gives identity to a fraction of the more than 400 local lives lost to the virus to date.
            </p>
           </a>

            <h3 class="article-card__headline" title="The Year of COVID: Windsor-Essex stats show stark difference between COVID, flu">
             <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
              The Year of COVID: Windsor-Essex stats show stark difference between COVID, flu
             </span>
            </h3>
            <p class="article-card__excerpt">
             Despite calls from some to label COVID-19 as simply a bad flu, the most recent available data from Public Health Ontario and the Windsor-Essex County Health Unit show the number of documented influenza cases and deaths since 2015 pale in comparison to novel coronavirus infections and deaths in the first year alone, from March 20, 2020, to March 19, 2021.
            </p>

            <a aria-label="They kill jobs, overwhelm treasuries, harm mental health but COVID lockdowns work, science suggests" class="article-card__link" href="/news/they-kill-jobs-overwhelm-treasuries-harm-mental-health-but-covid-lockdowns-work-science-suggests">

              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">

              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">

            <a aria-label="Reader letter: Inadequate government health care investment revealed during pandemic" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/letters/reader-letter-inadequate-government-health-care-investment-revealed-during-pandemic">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Reader letter: Inadequate government health care investment revealed during pandemic">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Reader letter: Inadequate government health care investment revealed during pandemic
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              The federal government recently announced billions of dollars for transportation which is definitely needed.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">
              Reader Letters
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__time">
              1hour ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">

           <a aria-label="Reader letter: Inadequate government health care investment revealed during pandemic" class="article-card__image-link" href="/opinion/letters/reader-letter-inadequate-government-health-care-investment-revealed-during-pandemic" tabindex="-1">
            <picture class="article-card__image">

            <a aria-label="Guest column: Vaccines will help, but we are long way off from full return to normal" class="article-card__link" href="/opinion/letters/guest-column-vaccines-will-help-but-still-a-long-way-off-from-full-return-to-normal">
             <h3 class="article-card__headline text-size--extra-large--sm-up" title="Guest column: Vaccines will help, but we are long way off from full return to normal">
              <span class="article-card__headline-clamp">
               Guest column: Vaccines will help, but we are long way off from full return to normal
              </span>
             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              Perhaps despite our wishes, hopes and expectations elected politicians cannot halt, stop or otherwise impede the insidious ooze of COVID-19 RNA viruses.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__author">
              Lloyd Brown-John
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__time">

             </h3>
             <p class="article-card__excerpt">
              CBD supplier sees five-year partnership as further signalling to athletes that UFC wants to play a prominent role in helping to educate them on CBD use.
             </p>
            </a>
            <div class="article-card__meta-bottom">
             <span class="article-card__time">
              2days ago
             </span>
             <span class="article-card__category">
              <a class="article-card__category-link" href="https://www.thegrowthop.com/category/cannabis-sports/">
               <span>
                Sports
               </span>
              </a>
             </span>
            </div>
           </div>
           <a aria-label="UFC names U.K.-based Love Hemp as its official global CBD partner" class="article-card__image-link" href="https://www.thegrowthop.com/cannabis-sports/ufc-names-u-k-based-love-hemp-as-its-official-global-cbd-partner" rel="noopener" tabindex="-1" target="_blank">
